=====DATABASE YANG DIUBAH=====
ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_users` ✅

CREATE table `leadspeak_business_resources`
- id BIGINT UNSIGNED autoincrement
- type ENUM('industry','crm','campaign_type','customer_list_source')
- slug VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT NULL
- name VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL
- label VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL
- description TEXT DEFAULT NULL
- created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL
- updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL

CREATE TABLE `leadspeek_business` ✅
- id BIGINT UNSIGNED autoincrement
- leadspeek_api_id VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL -> jangan lupa samakan collate nya di sandbox dan live
- website VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL -> Website
- business_type_id INT UNSIGNED -> Campaign Type
- business_name varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL -> Campaign name
- business_industry_id INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL -> Business industry
- business_specify VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL -> Please specify your industry
- business_description TEXT DEFAULT NULL -> What does your business do?
- business_competitors TEXT DEFAULT NULL -> Who are your main competitors?
- upload_customer_list_ids INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL -> How would you like to upload your customer list?
- crm_id INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL -> Connect your CRM
- crm_key TEXT DEFAULT NULL -> CRM API Key
- created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL
- updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL

CREATE TABLE `leadspeek_customers`
- id BIGINT UNSIGNED autoincrement
- user_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL
- customer_list_name VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL
- total_customer INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL
- url VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL
- size_file INT UNSIGNED INT DEFAULT NULL
- created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL
- updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL

CREATE TABLE `leadspeek_customer_campaigns` ✅
- id BIGINT UNSIGNED autoincrement
- leadspeek_api_id VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL -> jangan lupa samakan collate nya di sandbox dan live
- customer_id INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL
- created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL
- updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NULL

=====DATABASE YANG DIUBAH=====

- What does your business do? -> business_description (ALTER TEXT)
- Who are your main competitors? -> business_competitors (ALTER TEXT)

CREATE TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` (
  `id` BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `leadspeek_api_id` VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_download` TEXT DEFAULT NULL,
  `report_date` DATETIME DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` TIMESTAMP NULL,
  `updated_at` TIMESTAMP NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `leadspeek_predict_reports_pk` PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

  `id` BIGINT UNSIGNED NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
  `leadspeek_api_id` VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_download` TEXT DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` ENUM('found', 'not_found') DEFAULT NULL,
  'start_date' DATETIME NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  'end_date' DATETIME NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

SELECT
	id,
	company_id,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_name), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_name,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_value), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_value,
	setting_name,
	setting_value
FROM company_settings
WHERE company_id = 22 and CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_name), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) = 'rootdefaultmodules';

(campaign.payment_status != 'failed' || $store.getters.userData.manual_bill == 'T') && ( campaign.active_user == 'F' || (campaign.disabled == 'T' && campaign.active_user == 'T'))

	id,
	company_id,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_name), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_name,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_value), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_value,
	setting_name,
	setting_value
FROM company_settings
WHERE CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_name), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) = 'rootexistclientmoduleselect';

    public function getCustomersById(string $leadspeek_api_id)
    {
        info(__FUNCTION__, ['leadspeek_api_id' => $leadspeek_api_id]);
        $customers = LeadspeekCustomerCampaign::from('leadspeek_customer_campaigns as lcc')
            ->select(
                'lcc.id',
                'lcc.customer_list_name as name',
                'lcc.total_customer as total',
                'lcc.size_file',
                'lcc.url',
                DB::raw("DATE_FORMAT(lcc.created_at, '%Y-%m-%d') as date")
            )
            ->join('leadspeek_customers as lc', 'lc.id', '=', 'lcc.customer_id')
            ->where('lcc.leadspeek_api_id', $leadspeek_api_id)
            ->get();
        info(__FUNCTION__, ['customers' => $customers]);

        if($customers->count() == 0){
            return ['result' => 'error', 'message' => 'Customer not found'];
        }

        return ['result' => 'success', 'customers' => $customers];
    }

            this.$global.globalviewmode
        ) &&
        !this.$global.systemUser &&
        this.$global.creditcardsetup &&

AGENCY:
1. Tidak ada default price untuk setup fee dan monthly fee predictID untuk client (jika sudah dibuat saya rasa di hide aja), untuk setup fee dan monthly fee step 4 akan selalu $0 waktu create campaign ✅

5. Campaign ada tombol play dan stop, dimana kalau stop ada 2 opsi : (progress 4) 
    a. Akan langsung berhenti 
    b. Akan lanjut repotnya sampai next billing 

CLIENT:
1. Client hanya bisa download ✅
2. Client tidak bisa play dan stop (tidak muncul) ✅
3. Client tetep bisa liat detilnya ✅

TAMBAHAN:

2. Scenario untuk module agreement pop up

        a. Agree and Decline 
        b. Kalau agree otomatis akan charge monthly feenya, jika tidak / decline akan tetap seperti ini jika di klik 

    Jika Root tiba tiba ganti harga ataupun setting yg berubah dengan financial untuk module tersebut, maka ketika agency klik module tersebut akan ada pop up again dengan agreement yg baru, tapi pilihannya berbeda: 
        a. "Agree" berarti dia setuju dengan harga baru dan segala perubahannya 
        b. "Remain at Current Subscription" semua perubahan di balikan ke aslinya dan module tetep jalan 

    Jadi dia mau jawab agree atau tidak dua2nya tidak akan mendisabled menu yg sudah jalan

	id,
	company_id,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_name), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_name,
	CONVERT(AES_DECRYPT(FROM_bASE64(setting_value), '8e651522e38256f2') USING utf8mb4) as setting_value,

	setting_value

ADD COLUMN `available_contacts` bigint UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT 0
AFTER `final_expression`;


====== DATABASE YANG DIUBAH ======
ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` 
ADD `job_status` ENUM('pending', 'processing', 'done') NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `total_leads`, 
ADD `job_total` INT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_status`, 
ADD `job_completed` INT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_total`;

ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` CHANGE `total_leads` `total_leads` BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT '0';

CREATE TABLE leadspeek_predict_export_chunks (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    predict_reports_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    leadspeek_api_id VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL,
    chunk_index BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    offset BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    file_path TEXT DEFAULT NULL,
    row_count BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` ADD `workflow_id` TEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_completed`;
ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` ADD `merge_job_dispatched` TINYINT NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `workflow_id`;

ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` 
ADD `job_status` ENUM('pending', 'processing', 'done') NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `total_leads`, 
ADD `job_total` INT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_status`, 
ADD `job_completed` INT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_total`;

ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` CHANGE `total_leads` `total_leads` BIGINT UNSIGNED NULL DEFAULT '0';

CREATE TABLE leadspeek_predict_export_chunks (
    id BIGINT UNSIGNED AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    predict_reports_id BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    leadspeek_api_id VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL,
    chunk_index BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    offset BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    file_path TEXT DEFAULT NULL,
    row_count BIGINT UNSIGNED DEFAULT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` ADD `workflow_id` TEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `job_completed`;
ALTER TABLE `leadspeek_predict_reports` ADD `merge_job_dispatched` TINYINT NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `workflow_id`;

        # report masih berjalan sampai tanggal ulang tahun selanjutnya

* tentang cronojob anniversary agency predict
    - acuannya mengikuti dari awal anniversary agency, tidak ada kaitannya dengan anniversary report ataupun campaign
    - bakal nge reset PredictQuotaCampaigns
    - bakal nge charge agency
    - kondisi ketika agency gagal bayar (ini hold dulu nanti dipertanyakan)
        # misal gini agency agree tanggal 01Jan26, kemudian dia buat campaign #123456 di tanggal 15Jan26, kemudian saat memperbarui pembayaran di 01Feb2026 dia gagal charge, nah otomatis campaign #123456 akan di stop.
        # nah di tanggal misal 05Feb26, agency mulai melakukan memperbarui pembayaran, dan tanggal subscription dimulai dari tanggal 05Feb2026. nah disini lah inti topiknya, menurut saya campaign #123456 stop dari tanggal 01Feb26, seharusnya campaign bukan stop dalam mode (stop sekarang) ataupun (stop namun masih mendapatkan report sampai tanggal ulang tahun berikutnya), namun ketika agency play campaign #123456 lagi maka melakukan check, jika campaign di start belum lewat dari tanggal 15Feb26 maka jangan di charge, namun kalo misalnya sudah lewat dari 15Feb26 maka di charge.
        # dilemanya adalah ketika kita stop campaign #123456 dengan mode (stop namun masih mendapatkan report sampai tanggal ulang tahun berikutnya), itu ngga enak di emm, namun enak di client, sedangkan agency nya saja gagal bayar. menurut saya gapapa melakukan langkah tersebut, dan kalo seandainya client nya marah, maka yang pertama kali disalahkan pasti agency nya bukan emm. karena agency nya gagal bayar

* tentang cronjob anniversary campaign predict
    - acuannya mengikuti dari awal anniversary campaign, tidak ada kaitannya dengan anniversary agency ataupun report

* tentang overage campaign
    - misal gini agency agree tanggal 01Jan26 dengan (price_month = $10 dan max_campaigns = 1), dan langsung membuat 1 campaign. nah di tanggal 15Jan26 agency request ke emm, dia mau minta untuk max_campaigns nya jadi 2 dong. nah di posisi seperti ini agency tinggal ubah (price_month = $20 dan max_campaigns = 2), nah maka cara hitung nya gini, agency yang sudah dibuat kan 1, nah sisanya berarti (2 - 1 = 1). berarti harga yang dia bayar untuk penambahan campaign tersebut adalah $10. nah namun karena dia mulai dari tanggal 15Jan26, maka 15Jan26 sampai 01Feb26 kira" kalo kita pakai persentase durasi nya hanya 50% saja. maka dalam case ini dia membayar ($10 * 50% = $5)

Feb 02

Logic
First check the active / play campaign Second check created campaign that month
This more quota per month

balance : 20
harga : 260
auto topup : 250
total_balance : 20 + 250 = 270
sisa_balance : 270 - 260 = 10
topup_lagi : 250
total_balance : 10 + 250 = 260

days_diff = now − agree_date
weeks_passed = floor(days_diff / 7)
remaining_ratio = max(0, (4 − weeks_passed) / 4)

- sudah jalan 2 minggu (50%)
- yang harus dibayar = (price per campaign) * (sisa campaign) *  (persentase)
                     = ($10) * (4) *  (50%)
                     = $20

Calculations
1. harga per campaign nya jadi ($50 / 5) = $10
2. sisa campaign yang belum dibayar = 5 - 1 = 4
3. sudah jalan 2 minggu (50%)
4. yang harus dibayar = (price per campaign) * (sisa campaign) *  (persentase)
                      = ($10) * (4) *  (50%)
                      = $20

Calculations
1. The new price per campaign is ($50 / 5) = $10
2. Number of campaigns not yet paid for: 5 - 1 = 4
3. Time remaining in the billing period: 2 weeks (50%)
4. Amount to be paid = (price per campaign) × (remaining campaigns) × (percentage of time left)
                     = ($10) × (4) × (50%)
                     = $20
